        org.junit.Assert.assertTrue("'" + int8 + "' != '" + 0 + "'", int8 == 0);
        org.junit.Assert.assertTrue("'" + int9 + "' != '" + (-1) + "'", int9 == (-1));
        org.junit.Assert.assertTrue("'" + boolean10 + "' != '" + true + "'", boolean10 == true);
